						has_tech = modern_gmo

							has_tech = gene_therapy
						}

						chance = 50

					}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BLR_Communism_start"
			country_event = { id = belarus_character.5 days = 1 }
			hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = BLR_belarus_kommi_modifier } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = { localization_key = adds_dynamic_modifier_tt MODIFIER = BLR_belarus_kommi_modifier }
			add_to_variable = { BLR_belarus_kommi_political_power_gain = 0.01 tooltip = political_power_gain_tt }
			hidden_effect = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = BLR_AUTH_S_communism
				clr_country_flag = dynamic_flag
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = BLR_unstable_national_currency4
					}
					remove_ideas = BLR_unstable_national_currency4
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = farmers
					add_idea = communist_cadres
				}
				recalculate_party = yes
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } } }
					set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 4 }
					change_ruling_party_effect = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.45 }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.45 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Tatiana  Golubeva"
				picture = "tacciana_holubiewa.dds"
				ideology = Communist-State
				traits = {
					emerging_Communist-State
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 150
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				has_global_flag = BLR_COMMUNISM_PATH
			}
		}
	}
